National Goods Forum

The Mission of China National Goods Company 192

— Pan

In this national goods movement, the financial and industrial sectors, in order to seek active construction, have established China National Goods Company. This is not only an important record of national goods, but also a worthy record in the history of the national goods movement in China. This seems to be just a cooperative business in terms of sales, but it is also the first step in production and sales cooperation. Therefore, the National Goods Company really bears a significant mission in the future of the national goods movement.

Those in charge of the National Goods Company this time are mostly leaders with real strength in the industrial and commercial sectors. In terms of implementation, of course, there will be detailed and perfect plans to meet the expectations of the city's citizens. However, this National Goods Company is not only attracting attention from all industries and regions, but also the success or failure of this company is greatly related to the reputation of the national goods industry. Therefore, while we hope that fellow citizens will be determined to use national goods and do their best to cultivate this emerging national goods industry, we also hope that the colleagues of the National Goods Company will have the determination to serve and sacrifice, and engage in this business with a significant mission.

Regarding the determination to manage the business, because of the close interests involved, people will naturally work hard in their positions. They will also understand that this is a social undertaking, be more vigilant, reduce all bad prejudices, and enhance the status of our national goods. As for all the comrades serving in the company, they must eliminate all bad behavior and cultivate the ethos of model employees, because the loss of a customer by an ordinary store is only the loss of one store, while the loss of the National Goods Company will affect the entire national goods industry!

In the past, we were saddened and angered by the fact that ordinary merchants specialized in selling imported goods, but they all replied that national goods were not easy to sell. Now that the National Goods Company, which specializes in selling national goods, has opened, this is certainly an opportunity for our national goods production sector to examine and improve itself, and it is also an opportunity for ordinary merchants to test the sales of national goods. Moreover, in recent times, leaders in the industrial and commercial sectors in Chongqing, Qingdao, Shantou, and other places are all carrying out this business. The success or failure of our Shanghai efforts is really enough to affect their actions. Therefore, the National Goods Company is not only a new business in the national goods movement, but also the central business of the national goods movement. We should do our best to manage it. In particular, everyone must have a sense of responsibility, self-confidence, and willingness to sacrifice. Don't just do it for yourself, do it for others. Don't just take care of private business, take care of the overall situation. Don't just focus on sales, pay attention to production. Don't just benefit the production sector, but also consider the consumer.

This is certainly just the beginning of cooperation on the sales front, but it is also the starting point for production and sales cooperation. We must lay the foundation this time in order to engage in future large-scale cooperation in production, purchasing, and other aspects with the same industry. Therefore, both internally and externally, for the sake of the entire national goods movement, we should pay attention to the China National Goods Company and support the China National Goods Company at all times.

Interview Notes

Mr. Wu Yun Chu Talks About the Record of the Completion of European and American Surveys 193

Mr. Wu Yun Chu is an authority in China's chemical industry. While monosodium glutamate has certainly established his achievements and status, in recent years he has also been engaged in the electrical industry, standing in a leading position in the emerging national goods industrial and commercial circles, and catching up head-on in the international production circles as well. His intelligence and vision are truly admirable. However, Mr. Wu himself has never been complacent with the current situation. Therefore, he went to Europe and America for further investigation last year. This spirit of research and progress is still rarely seen in our industrial and commercial circles. Mr. Wu returned to China a few months ago, and the reporter went to the Tianchu Factory to pay a visit. He talked about his various feelings from this trip, many of which can be used as a reference for our industrial and commercial circles, so I will introduce them later.

Mr. Wu's purpose for going abroad this time was to conduct technical investigations. He visited 73 factories in countries such as Japan, the United States, Britain, France, Italy, and Belgium, including electrical, green gas, alkali burning, gelatin, and starch industries. They were all closely related to the businesses that Mr. Wu is currently running. Mr. Wu paid more attention to the light gas and fiber chemical industries that he was designing this time during his investigations, and he studied them at all times. Now the drawings and plans have been completed. Mr. Wu kept a detailed diary during this trip. Because there were more records on technical aspects, the reporter only talked to Mr. Wu about some of his impressions from this trip, especially those related to our Chinese national goods industrial and commercial circles.

Regarding production, according to Mr. Wu's observation, since 1929, due to the progress of machinery and scientific management, foreign countries have gone from a shortage of labor to an overproduction, forming the current wave of unemployment. However, regarding the chemical industry, among the many factories in Europe, labor is still used more often because it is more accurate. Therefore, our emerging national goods production sector should not repeat the mistakes of others and blindly follow trends when it comes to machinery. There are also many old machines in foreign factories, and they have not been discarded but are still being used for production. Our Chinese people's erroneous concepts should also be eliminated. Regarding the issue of production raw materials, the United States, which advocates mass production, sometimes inevitably wastes them. France, on the other hand, treasures even scraps of wood and carefully stores them, and even garbage has a use. It uses heat as power, and slag as building materials, without wasting anything.

What is especially shocking to us is that modern warfare has already become a war of materials. In addition to ordinary production, industrial circles in various countries must also take into account the use of national defense. Not only is the police already militarized like the national defense army, but also ordinary factories丨famous ones such as Germany's Krupp and France's Schneider丨can be converted into arsenals at any time. In this environment full of national disasters, seeing others' deep planning and foresight, and thinking about our own lack of preparation, what kind of feelings should we have? This point really cannot but be reported to our national goods production sector.

Therefore, based on the stimulation given by others, Mr. Wu decided to abandon production with greater profits and start working on green gas and light gas. It is said that light gas is an important raw material for explosives and a necessity for national defense, but in the process of undertaking

The Enamel Department of China National Goods Company 194

Inscription for China National Goods Company: Cherish National Goods 195

— Shi Liangcai

My Thoughts on the National Goods Company 196

— Tianxu Wosheng

The Chinese National Goods Company of the Mainland Business District opened today. I had just returned to Shanghai from Wuxi, and because I wasn't very clear on the specific details, I thought it was some kind of joint organization of the Nine Factories. It wasn't until January 6th that I learned the goods sold weren't limited to the Nine Factories. Any product produced by a national goods factory is welcome to be sent for display and consignment. Therefore, I quickly sent various products of the "Invincible" brand to participate, and I have a few thoughts as follows:

From the manufacturer's perspective, there has always been a perceived difficulty in display and distribution. Setting up one's own store often feels monotonous because the items sold are too limited, not as diverse as a small department store. So, it often amounts to nothing. As a result, there are more stores opening than buyers, and even covering rent and food expenses with both principal and interest is insufficient, inevitably leading to closure. Regarding pricing, it is even more challenging. Clearly, a one-dollar item, wholesaled to other businesses, is only a few cents or fractions of a cent, but in one's own retail store, it's impossible to sell it at the wholesale price. Otherwise, the retailer would have no profit, and would demand a discount, shaking the original established position. However, from the retailer's perspective, there's room for flexibility. For example, during a big sale, they often deliberately sacrifice a bit on a popular and valuable item to attract customers, and then make a substantial profit on other goods to compensate. Under such circumstances, the price of the same item sold in one's own store must not be lower than the general reduced price, which will cause buyers to question, thinking that the factory's goods are more expensive than elsewhere. This will be spread by word of mouth, and will instead harm the buyer's goodwill, creating a reverse advertisement. Now that there is a National Goods Company that can handle the display and distribution, it can avoid setting up one's own retail store. This is a great convenience for us manufacturers. I hope that manufacturers everywhere quickly send all of their products to the company for consignment, as boldly as possible. In any case, the effectiveness of this kind of physical advertisement must be greater than any other form of advertising. And from the buyer's perspective, they will feel that everything is available, without the regret of something missing. For example, if a buyer comes in wanting to buy a certain product of brand A, but it is not available, they will reluctantly try and buy the same product of brand B. If the brand B product is indeed good, the buyer's trust will naturally shift from A to B, and they will definitely choose B over A in the future. This kind of shift in trust, with one gain and one loss on both sides of A and B, has a significant impact on the future of the business. So, I think that any manufacturer who has a product must not lag behind and fail to join. For the National Goods Company, seeking to promote national goods as its goal, universally soliciting products is also a very important task, because no matter how much or little business a buyer does, all expenses add up. If someone comes specifically to buy a certain item, but searches the entire place and can't find it, they will naturally not bother asking, and leave disappointed, blaming themselves for going to the wrong place, and not coming back again. Then business will gradually become slow, and from where will the expenses come? So I think the company must solicit universally. If there are well-known and popular national goods that are not immediately available, they should buy a small amount with cash to meet the needs of buyers, so that they won't leave disappointed. I think that buying goods with cash will definitely get extra discounts. The company gets extra discounts, and buyers can also get extra discounts. This is a natural public principle. I hope that the same product is not limited to being sold by the same merchant. Even if the price varies, the buyer's result will be cheaper compared to buying it elsewhere. Then word of mouth will spread, and even if the threshold of the National Goods Company is made of steel, it will be worn down!

Speech

The Spirit That Those Engaged in the National Goods Business Should Possess 197

Chi Junzong is one of the founders of the Tongcheng Textile Company. He had many plans for the establishment of the company. Recently, Chi Jun spoke at the China National Goods Production and Sales Cooperative Association on [The Spirit That Those Engaged in the National Goods Business Should Possess]. His words were long and heartfelt, with unique insights. I recorded them here as a motto for those engaged in industry (Guangqian Record).

The factory I run deals with fly waste. It was only ten years ago that factories began to engage in this business. The raw materials are the waste from cotton yarn factories, such as fly waste and oil waste. Ten years ago, ordinary yarn factories did not know how to use the fly waste and sold it to foreign merchants to be shipped abroad, spun into yarn, and woven into cloth before being sold back to China, resulting in countless outflows of profits. Later, the Shanghai Minsheng Yarn Factory, in light of this, took the initiative to launch this industry, and our factory followed suit. We purchased machines from Germany to start the business. I was not originally involved in industry, but as a representative of the bank, I held the position of deputy manager. At that time, spinning yarn from oil waste did not yield good results. In addition, the Qilu War in the thirteenth year of the Republic of China caused business to be sluggish and sales to be stagnant, and the capital turnover was not smooth, leading to a sudden failure. The following year, we reopened the factory, determined to reorganize, and actually spun the yarn and built the new factory building. Everything progressed quite smoothly. Unexpectedly, the revolutionary army rose in the sixteenth year of the Republic of China, causing temporary chaos and almost undoing all previous efforts. After some reorganization, we were able to slightly restore the old appearance. At that time, we only knew how to manufacture scarves, Luzon hats, and socks, but I always wanted to make the most of the materials and make cloth. Later, I went to a foreign firm and bought a machine to study how to make wool. At first, the wool we made was of poor quality and unsightly. After exhausting our efforts and working hard to study, we were able to make wearable wool. Gradually, we were able to manufacture flannel and felt. Now, all of our products have suitable patterns and are available in all colors, which was beyond our imagination when we first started. During the research and manufacturing process, we encountered many difficulties due to insufficient capital. Fortunately, we were given a lot of care by all sectors, which enabled us to achieve success. We encountered a setback when manufacturing military felt. At that time, the Ministry of Military Affairs did not believe that the military felt made by the Chinese themselves was sufficient for use. Later, the Commodity Inspection Bureau conducted a chemical test, and the results showed that our products were excellent, pure in texture, and free of oil, surpassing imported products. At this point, the authorities began to believe that the national goods industry had made great progress, and our products also gained a good reputation as a result. As for the flannel we make, a certain foreigner told me that it was on par with Japanese goods. This may be an exaggeration, but it is a happy and satisfying thing that waste materials can now be utilized.

However, I still have something to regret. In the ten years of operation, we have only made two products, flannel and felt. Therefore, I have the following feelings:

(1) Those engaged in national goods are bound to fail at first, and must try again after failure. Looking at Liu Bang in Chinese history, he was defeated and fought repeatedly, and finally defeated the Chu tyrant and established the world. Those engaged in national goods should have this "tumbler" spirit. After falling, come again, and come even more after falling. Never give up, never give up, and eventually there will be a day of success. However, the business can fail, but the personality cannot fail, because personality is the soul of the business. Once the personality is gone, even if there is a way to turn the tide, the business will never have hope of success.

(2) Chinese people often have the three words "almost there" in their minds, and these three words are the enemy of success. Every time, a small difference leads to a big mistake. Those who run industries must not have the "almost there" mentality. Every matter and every thing should be carefully investigated step by step. When problems arise, they should not be tired of details, and they should study them carefully from a long-term perspective. This is not only the capital for success, but also a way to prevent the source of failure. (3) Those who run industries must not be afraid of trouble. If a factory is afraid of trouble and wants to achieve quick success and simplicity in everything, there will be big problems. Therefore, those who run industries should not only not be afraid of trouble, but also look for troublesome things to do. The more troublesome, the more they should study and do it, because the more you are afraid of trouble, the more trouble will find you, and the more troublesome things will become. Troublesome things, if done at the beginning, will no longer be troublesome, and if not done, they will become lifelong troubles. Clearly, those who run factories will not encounter any problems.

(4) Those who run industries should learn from the spirit of [Tang Seng's journey to obtain scriptures], gather talents widely, and work together in harmony. A person like Tang Seng, who is so gentle and refined and likely to fall over in the wind, went to Tibet to obtain scriptures. The journey was long and full of monsters, which was originally an impossible task. However, because he had Sun Wukong, Zhu Bajie, and Sha Monk following him, working together with one heart and one mind, and faithfully protecting him along the way, he finally achieved his goal. Running a factory is like Tang Seng going to Tibet to obtain scriptures because of a difficult task, but if there are talents like Sun Wukong, Zhu Bajie, and Sha Monk who join in, work hard and willingly, and do things loyally and courageously, there will be achievements.

(5) Those engaged in the national goods business must have the greatest determination. Chinese people often say: [Nothing is difficult in the world, only those who are afraid of having a heart], and also say: [Where the spirit reaches, metal and stone will open]. Those engaged in the national goods business must have this determination to fight, and always keep national goods in mind, and then they can make national goods, make good national goods, and make national goods that are happy to use. (6) Now, foreign-run businesses have sophisticated technology, good management, and strong capital. Those engaged in the national goods business must have some courage to compete with them. Hundreds of years ago, there was a business group in Europe who felt that the sun was very annoying and vowed to invent something to cover it. China also had the story of [Yugong removing mountains]. These things seem very absurd, but those who run national goods factories should have this courage. If they can't do it well in their own lives, let their children and grandchildren do it, and there will be a day of success. If you want to calculate when it will definitely succeed, this matter will never succeed.

In peacetime, it can manufacture salt and nitrate (for fertilizing fields). The machines can also manufacture Methanal (gasoline substitute), and will not lose sales because there is no war.

Overseas Chinese in the Americas, because of the continuous years of war and banditry in the country, mostly have a "enjoy here, don't think about tomorrow" mentality abroad. Although everyone is very sympathetic to investing in and developing industries in the motherland, they are given a very bad impression because of the dangers of kidnapping, etc., and the fact that overseas Chinese have invested heavily in several businesses in the past, and the results have been disastrous. Mr. Wu solemnly said to the reporter, "If we want overseas Chinese to return to the country to serve the country's production sector, our business can only succeed in the future, and there can be no more failures. This is the only way to establish credibility." Finally, talking about recent events in Japan, we can learn from them and tell us a shocking message!

[In this Shanghai battle, Japan also felt that the aircraft shell picric acid was not good, and decided to change to a mixture of perchlorate NH6CIO4 and wood chips, heavy oil ferrosilicon FeSi; now, in order to encourage the people to manufacture, the government pays 1,200 yuan for items with a cost of 350 yuan per ton, and many factories are working day and night to manufacture them. (Note: ferrosilicon Ees, with Therneal properties, can start fires.)]

This is indeed the ambition of the aggressor, but what about us who are being invaded? Are we just waiting to die? Our conversation stopped at this time, but this deep impression still lingered in my mind.

Trench Life and Loving National Goods 198

— Yinge

What is trench life like? The military uniform you wear is naturally unchangeable and is made of dirty wool, as filthy, damp, and cold as possible, and you must endure it. The coarse food and cold dishes you eat are enough to fill you up. You can't sleep soundly day and night, or because you are extremely tired, you fall asleep leaning on the mud bed, only to be awakened again by the sound of artillery and bombs.

The small room supported by wood or iron sheets, the small room protected by mud and sandbags, is constantly destroyed by artillery shells or bombs. The rumbling of artillery and bombs, and the rustling falling of mud, are the only decorations in the trenches.

You don't want to use national goods, saying that this thing is not good to wear, not good to eat, and not comfortable to use. You must say that imported goods are good, and even say that Japanese goods are good. Think about what life is like for patriotic soldiers in the trenches? To be honest, there are all kinds of national goods to wear, eat, and use, but they are indeed not as beautiful and comfortable as foreign goods. But if we can often think of the food, clothing, and shelter in the trenches, then it doesn't matter if it's not beautiful or comfortable!

How National Goods Should Seek a Way Out Under Heavy Pressure (4) 200

— Du Chongyuan

Regarding the vertical aspect: 1. Restricting imports, 2. Abolishing all exorbitant taxes, 3. Transportation without obstacles: 4. Government assistance. The first three are what our government has been striving for day and night, but have not yet been realized. If our domestic politics continue to be so chaotic, then at least in the short term, they cannot be realized. As for the last point, if politics is on the right track, there is no problem, but under this kind of situation, it is not absolutely impossible. To remedy the above points, we can only do it ourselves. How to do it? First, use propaganda methods to arouse the concept of people happily using national goods. In recent years, domestic industrial products have made rapid progress. All products can indeed be compared with imported products, and some have even surpassed foreign products, but because the Chinese people have been surrounded by foreign goods for a long time, they have a despicable traditional concept and always doubt that national goods cannot catch up with foreign goods. Even better national goods are often mistaken for foreign goods. If the national goods factory industry can use propaganda, on the one hand, inform the people of the crisis of foreign economic invasion in China: on the other hand, clarify the national duty of using national goods, and sincerely promote it to the people in the way of evangelism. At the same time, national goods display places should be set up in all commercial ports and cities and towns to arouse the people's interest and recognition of using national goods. It is even more regrettable that all public entertainment is held in national goods display places, improving all bad habits of the people, and instilling new knowledge in the people, so that the people develop a sense of conscience and disgust for foreign goods and reject them unanimously. If this is done conscientiously, then this power is indeed very great. Secondly, the production sector and the consumer sector should work together to abolish exorbitant taxes in order to reduce the cost of the production sector, which indirectly reduces the burden on consumers. Thirdly, in terms of transportation, we should now choose places that foreign goods can reach as the first step in promoting national goods, and it is not very difficult to gradually enter towns and villages.

The Russian People's Love for National Goods 201

— Mingfeng

Kunshan Zhou Tongqing returned to China from his country via Europe and stayed briefly in Moscow. According to him, the Russians use all national goods. The magnetic basin used in the hotel is not very good in quality, but it is all national goods. The Russian paper-making industry has not yet developed, and the paper produced is not enough to meet the demand. Therefore, the paper used for invoices issued by stores is almost equivalent to Chinese rough paper. Mr. Zhou even brought one back to China as a souvenir. I wonder what the Chinese who love imported goods think about this?

Russian customs are extremely strict. If you have not purchased Russian goods, you cannot seek sales in Russia. And you must use goods of equal price to offset each other.

Our country's customs cannot be completely autonomous. However, if everyone can check themselves, if they cannot produce export goods, they will never use imported goods, then imported goods will inevitably be sharply reduced. For example, most ordinary people cannot produce or sell goods overseas, then they have no right to purchase foreign goods. I often see people who cannot earnestly study and focus on production, and they are happy to buy foreign goods and claim to be open-minded. This kind of person is the root of national destruction and family ruin.

Sales Problems Under Scientific Management 202

— Cheng Shouzhong's Speech at Qiacheng Ji

First: The national goods business community should have a kind of union. The benefits of union are of course well known to all of you, and there is no need to repeat them; the merger of Mr. Liu Hongsheng's match and enamel factory and the merger of Kangyuan Canning Factory and other canning factories are enough to prove the trend and need for union. As for the method of union, there are two types, one is the union of the same industry, and the other is the union of various industries: after the union, the following important work can be done:

(1) Research work: study how to classify, because after classification can you understand what goods to send to where to sell, special to special, ordinary to ordinary, sales can be convenient, and the sales channels of our current business community seem to have gone wrong, and they have suffered a lot. Regarding this issue, I will do another article to discuss it, and I will not repeat it now.

(2) After the same industry is united, all aspects of sales, advertising, and purchasing raw materials can be carried out jointly, and manpower and financial resources will be more economical at the same time. Second: China's current market organization is not very sound. Financial institutions and industry and commerce lack contact, which affects the sales of national goods. Mr. Yang has advocated on this issue in the National Goods Weekly of Shen Bao, and I am very much in favor of it. Secondly, China does not have wholesalers now, and even if there are a few, they are not sound. According to the statistics of the Shanghai Municipal Social Bureau, there are very few factories with more than 5,000 people, and there are many small factories; the capital of these many small factories is not very sufficient. If the wholesalers are sound, with the help of warehouses and finance, it will be a great help to these many small factories. They can completely hand over the responsibility of sales to the wholesalers, because most small factories are managed by one person, from purchasing raw materials to sales, they are all responsible by one person, and their energy is limited, so they must divide and cooperate, and small factories specialize in manufacturing, and wholesalers preside over sales, which is beneficial to both production and sales. I still ask all of you present today to discuss this idea in detail.

Third: Regarding the purchase of raw materials, the current manufacturers mostly buy from merchants and brokers. In fact, the sellers get very little, but the intermediaries get a lot of profit; we understand that most of the consumers of Chinese national goods are farmers. If we want to increase production, we must increase their consumption. In order to reduce the exploitation of the middleman and take care of the economy of the farmers, we should help them organize production and sales cooperation.

Fourth: Organize production and sales cooperative chain stores; recently, Shanghai is preparing to set up a national goods company, and I hope that it can take on this mission, that is, take the company in Shanghai as the starting point and form a chain of stores with companies in various places, and let this chain of stores be responsible for sales, customs declaration, and distribution.

Planning of Jiangsu Education Funds 204

Education Fund Management Office Urges Payment of Funds

Insufficient Funds for the Second Half of October

Although the payment notice for October for the provincial schools and social education institutions in Jiangsu Province has been received, at the end of the lunar year, each school only received half a month's payment. According to the usual practice, the counties in the lunar year have good harvests and there is more hope, but it is said that it has been affected by heavy snow and frozen rivers. For the first half of November, some schools received the full amount of the payment notice from the counties, while others only received half or several tenths. On average, they have received 70% to 80%. In addition, there are expenses for studying abroad in the East and West, about 30,000 yuan for the winter months (October, November, December), which has not been received yet. The reasons for the lack of funds are: first, the Finance Department has not paid the education funds from the counties and the provincial subsidies owed in the past; second, it is difficult for people to enter the city to complete and pay the grain due to the frozen rivers; and third, the Education Fund Management Office borrowed 200,000 yuan from the Jiangsu China Communications Bank, which was originally agreed to repay 100,000 yuan at the end of December and 100,000 yuan at the end of January. Later, because it could not be done on time, it was extended to repay 100,000 yuan at the end of January and 100,000 yuan at the end of February. It is said that 88,000 yuan of the 100,000 yuan at the end of January has been repaid. Currently, the balance in each bank is different, ranging from several thousand yuan. Recently, the frozen river has thawed, and the Management Office sent staff member Ni Dongfu to Yixing to urge the payment of funds (Yixing recently owes 20,000 to 30,000 yuan) and ordered each county or finance bureau that owes education funds to pay quickly in order to pay the insufficient funds for the second half of October for the provincial schools and the expenses for studying abroad, it is said.

Totaling 5,400 Silver Dollars for Three Months

Shanghai Education Bureau Director Pan Gongzhan's Lecture [Education in Shanghai] (I) 209

| Lecture given at the Shanghai YMCA on the evening of the 7th of this month |

An Overview of School and Social Education

The YMCA invited Pan Gongzhan, Director of the Shanghai Education Bureau, to give a lecture entitled "Education in Shanghai" at 9:15 PM the night before last (the 7th). Xie Fusheng translated. Although the content mainly consisted of statistical data, the audience did not feel bored, as they were all interested in education. Therefore, the lecture ended at 11:00 PM before the audience dispersed. Reporters from foreign newspapers such as the North-China Daily News and the China Press were also present to record the lecture. It is reported that the YMCA invited Mayor Wu to give a lecture on "The Municipality of Greater Shanghai" in December. Director Pan's lecture the night before last was essentially a part of "The Municipality of Greater Shanghai." In the future, the YMCA will continue to invite directors from various bureaus of the Municipal Government to give lectures. The record of Director Pan's speech is as follows:

Chairman, Ladies and Gentlemen,

We are currently in a time of national crisis. There are undoubtedly many important issues that are attracting public attention. However, I am grateful to the YMCA for giving me this wonderful opportunity to give a seemingly dry and uninteresting talk about education before you tonight. I feel ashamed and deeply grateful. I believe that you all have unlimited sympathy for the future of China and firmly believe that China's only hope lies in the universal education of the Chinese people. Shanghai has naturally become an important hub in China's overall improvement plan and will continue to shoulder the task of influencing and promoting progress in other parts of the country.

Speaking of Shanghai, since its opening as a trading port in 1843, it has made rapid progress. Now, Shanghai accounts for 40% of China's import and export trade. Moreover, due to the development of Shanghai's education, it has also formed a cultural center. In July 1917 (the 16th year of the Republic of China), the Shanghai Special Municipal Government was established, with a status equal to that of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, directly under the Central Government. The seventeen rural towns previously under the jurisdiction of Shanghai and Baoshan counties, including famous locations during last year's Songhu War of Resistance against Japan such as Zhabei, Wusong, Jiangwan, and Zhenru, were all placed under the jurisdiction of the Special Municipality. In July 1930 (the 19th year of the Republic of China), it was reorganized in accordance with the newly promulgated Municipal Organization Law and renamed Shanghai Municipality. The department under the Municipal Government in charge of education is the Shanghai Education Bureau, which I currently oversee. You can imagine that for a city with a population of 3.5 million, the taxes available for education are very limited, especially after the Shanghai War. With such a stretched-thin Education Bureau, how much of the work that should be done for the citizens of Greater Shanghai has actually been accomplished is self-evident.

In China, or on a smaller scale, in Shanghai alone, the development of education has not been based on a comprehensive plan. Therefore, upon investigating the history of various educational institutions, no consistent patterns have been found. Regardless of the size of the school, its establishment and operation are all independent. How to cooperate with each other depends on the appropriate opportunity. The sprout of new education in China is a reaction to the opening of the country to the outside world and contact with foreigners in the last hundred years. Knowing this, the unevenness and lack of coordination in education are not surprising. I would like to briefly describe the state of education in Shanghai within the time allotted, based on this point. Please forgive me for not understanding why the YMCA chose 9:15 PM as the lecture time. I'm afraid it will be close to 11:00 PM when I finish speaking. By then, everyone will be eager to go home and sing "Returning Home." There is no need to give such a bland lecture. However, this time is a fixed tradition, and traditions cannot be broken. I should stop talking nonsense and quickly summarize what I want to say into two sections:

1) An Overview of School Education | From elementary education to university.

2) An Overview of Social Education.

I hope to finish what I want to say within an hour, as the translation will also take the same amount of time. Due to the nature of the topic, I will inevitably use some statistical figures. Listening to numbers is like chewing wax. Please forgive me.

Let me first talk about school education. This includes elementary schools, middle schools, independent colleges, universities, kindergartens, and vocational schools. To understand the present, we must briefly describe the past.

The earliest elementary school was the Meixi Academy, established in 1878 (the fourth year of the Guangxu reign of the Qing Dynasty). The Yangzheng Academy was established in 1930. Jingye was founded by Magistrate Wang Maokun. The other two schools were initially founded by private individuals.

Among the middle schools, the earliest were the Binggong Middle School, established in 1863, the Xuhui Public School founded by the French Catholic Church, the Qingxin Middle School founded by the American Presbyterian Church, the Private Nanyang Middle School, and the Private YMCA Middle School. Other middle schools, such as Minli, Pudong, Chengzhong, and Mailun, were also established one after another.

The earliest normal school was the Normal College of Nanyang Public School in 1897. In 1904, Circuit Intendant Yuan Shuxun changed the Longmen Academy into the Longmen Normal School. At the end of the Qing Dynasty, normal training centers were established one after another, and then they were successively closed down. Only the one attached to the Wuben Women's School continued uninterrupted. After the establishment of the Republic of China, Longmen Normal School was renamed Jiangsu Provincial Second Normal School. In 1930, the Municipal Government established Xinlu Normal School as the most recently established normal school.

The formal vocational school was established by the China Vocational Education Society in 1918, starting with the China Vocational School.

The first formal kindergarten was not established until the establishment of the Municipal First Kindergarten in 1929, as kindergartens were previously attached to various elementary schools.

The above is just a brief overview of the history of primary and secondary schools in Shanghai. Now, I will briefly talk about the Shanghai Municipal Government's education funding, because the amount of funding is directly proportional to the success of the cause. Before the establishment of the Municipal Government, Shanghai's education funding was not fixed, mostly relying on land tax and a portion of house tax and miscellaneous taxes. In the event of a disaster or poor harvest, education funding would suffer. After the establishment of the Shanghai Municipal Government in 1927, the financial system implemented unified revenue and expenditure, which was a welcome reform. Education funding was stipulated to be 25% of the city's available revenue. According to the 1931 budget (from July 1931 to June 1932), although education funding did not reach 25% of the total revenue, it accounted for more than 1.2%. Now, if we compare the funding for 1927-1928 and 1931-1932, we can see the year-by-year progress of the education cause run by the Municipal Government.

1927-1928 1931-1932 Increase

Administrative Expenses 41,910.13 142,387.07 100,476.94

School Education 214,515.92 633,510.62 418,994.70

It has been almost a month since the Sun Yat-sen Cultural Education Center began preparations. Since the day before yesterday, a large number of publications donated by local bookstores such as Commercial Press, China Book Company, Pacific Bookstore, and Huiwentang have been received. Many other magazine publishers have also replied, promising to send donations regularly on a yearly basis. Now, a second batch of hundreds of solicitation letters has been sent to party departments, agencies, organizations, and universities at all levels across the country to solicit publications. Therefore, the staff of the committee have been working day and night, advancing with writing, and handling hundreds of documents every day. The original letter from the committee urging sponsors to pay donations is copied below: Respectfully, we believe that culture is the life of the nation, and the teachings of the late Dr. Sun Yat-sen are the foundation of the new cultural movement in our country, which urgently needs to be promoted and developed. Therefore, at the Third Plenary Session of the Central Committee, the establishment of the Sun Yat-sen Cultural Education Center was proposed. We are grateful to you for your initial support and signing as a sponsor. Your enthusiasm for culture is deeply appreciated. A preparatory committee has now been established at No. 10 Molier Road, Shanghai, to begin preparations, and it is expected to be officially established within two months. During this preparatory period, all facilities require funding, and the establishment fee urgently needs to be collected. According to the regulations, sponsors should donate an establishment fee of more than 500 yuan. We dare to write to you requesting that you immediately pay the donated establishment fee to the Shanghai Central China Communications National Overseas Chinese Shanghai Six Banks for collection and use. You are also requested to raise the foundation of more than 500 yuan in the specified period and pay it to the above-mentioned bank for safekeeping. A donation register is attached for your review.

Young Heroes Like Bamboo Shoots After Rain: The World of Tennis in 1933

America, Australia, Germany, France, South Africa, Spain

New Youngsters Create Amazing Results

Progress is Faster Than Expected

France to Employ New Players to Retain the Davis Cup 216

British tennis expert W. Myers discusses the world of tennis in 1933: "Looking around the world, in 1933, the brilliance of male and female tennis stars will be even more dazzling. It is unpredictable that someone like Vines will jump into the center court of Wimbledon and win the championship. At the very least, it will refresh the audience and amaze everyone. In the recent year, young heroes have emerged all over the world like bamboo shoots after rain. Their progress is faster than expected."

Australian McGrath 217

"The two young people from Australia and South Africa must be discussed first. Australia's V. McGrath is only seventeen years old. During the American tennis team's tour of Australia, he first defeated Allison and then Crawford. In the Australian Championships, he defeated Vines again. Vines's record of victory was 6-2, 2-6, 8-6, 7-5. Vines only won the second set, and the intensity of the competition can be imagined. However, he eventually lost to his compatriot Crawford. McGrath's skills must be as brave as he is. His two-handed backhand is even more accurate."

South African Bertram 218

"South Africa's M. Bertram from Johannesburg is slightly older than McGrath, but he is still new in the eyes of the world. He was a finalist in the South African Championships. As a talented tennis player, he has defeated South African stars Kerbell, Robbins, and Chenghasen. His movements are agile, and he is capable of everything. However, he recently lost to the Englishman Lee."

Two North American Youths 219

"Speaking of the United States, the most interesting are two. 1) O. Sutter, the All-American Collegiate Champion, will tour Europe this month and may reach southern France. Last year, he twice soundly defeated Austin. In the All-American Championships, he lost to Vines in a five-set battle. Vines was shocked. Sutter has the confidence that a champion must have. His passing shots are even more confident. He is one of the most promising people this year."

"K. CledLill is Vines's doubles partner and the runner-up in the All-American doubles. Although they lost to Allison and Van Hui, they later won back. His doubles is better than his singles. K is especially popular. The audience in the stadium likes him very much. Wimbledon is probably no exception. K is currently touring Australia."

German Cramm 220

"The most improved player in Europe in 1932 was Germany's C. VonCramm. Vines, Shields, and Austin can all tell you about his abilities. If Cramm gets Froizheim's inheritance, he can turn defeat into victory. The ferocity of his smash makes his lob shots even more impressive."

Spanish Manuel 221

"Another rising star in Europe to remember is Spain's Maiej. Manuel belongs to the Spanish army and is a soldier. His special point is that he only needs a short period of practice. With a month of effort, he can win six games. He defeated Barracura at Wimbledon last year. His overhead smash is especially moving."

Two French Youths 222

"France's two youths, M. Bernard and A. erlinM, will definitely achieve amazing results. Bernard is a left-handed player and is only twenty years old. He only appeared on the international stage last year. At the French Tennis Open, he was invincible all the way, and only lost to Cochian in the final."

"Bernard's style is completely champion-like. His weakness is only that he is too conservative. Bernard and Bowsers have been practicing doubles all winter. In the Davis Cup, they may replace Cochian and Browny."

"Merlin is a student of Cochian. Merlin's characteristic is that his shots do not seem to have decisive power, but his fierce attack often defeats the enemy. He ranks fourth in France, behind Barracura. Merlin will be the one to watch. It is only said that Merlin is too eager to win, but this kind of forward courage is a commendable mistake."

France Will Use New Players 223

(Paris News) France has won the Davis Cup from the United States since 1927. Now it has been six years. In the past six years, the players have been only Cochian, Lacoste, Barracura, and Browny. This year, new players will be employed. In addition to Cochian, one or two new young people will be selected to challenge the United States or other countries. Two of the three musketeers may retire this fall to be spectators when they retain the Davis Cup. There may only be Cochian in the French team, but the French still remember Cochian's two defeats to Fan Enqi. Lacoste, who was originally planned to be reused last year, can no longer revive. Barracura has decided to retire. The new players to be used will be Bernard or Herlin. Bernard and Bowers have been practicing cooperation for some time, and may replace the Cochian Browny team. But in any case, France's lineup, as in last year, will be finalized at the last minute.

Essays

Wu Dialect becoming Northernized 239

— Zhan Lu

Due to the convenience of transportation, the Wu dialect also contains some Northernized phrases; however, they are very few, accounting for only one or two percent.

First, there is the character [上] (shàng, up). In the Suzhou dialect, the character [上] (shàng) in phrases like 上門 (shàng mén, go to the door), 上山 (shàng shān, go up the mountain), and 上樓 (shàng lóu, go upstairs) is pronounced as the departing tone of the character 撞 (zhuàng, collide). However, when saying [馬上就去] (mǎ shàng jiù qù, go immediately), not only is the character [上] (shàng) pronounced in the Northern way, but even the character [馬] (mǎ, horse) is pronounced in the Northern way.

Second, there is the character [下] (xià, down). The character [下] (xià) in phrases like 下山 (xià shān, go down the mountain) and 下樓 (xià lóu, go downstairs) is pronounced in the local dialect; however, when saying [下不過去] (xià bù guò qù, can't get by), this character [下] (xià) is pronounced in the Northern way, sounding like 諧駕切一 (xié jià qiē yī).

Third, there is the character [玉] (yù, jade). The Suzhou dialect pronounces the character [玉] (yù) as a checked tone; the Northern dialect lacks checked tones, so the character [玉] (yù) is pronounced similar to [御] (yù, imperial). When Suzhou people say [玉官要買玉麥丨卽珍珠米] (yù guān yào mǎi yù mài | jí zhēnzhū mǐ, jade official wants to buy jade corn | that is, pearl rice); the [玉] (yù) in 玉官 (yù guān, jade official) is pronounced with a checked tone, while the [玉] (yù) in 玉麥 (yù mài, jade corn) is pronounced like [御] (yù, imperial), so the name 御麥 (yù mài, imperial corn) is also Northernized.

Fourth, there is the character [黃] (huáng, yellow). Suzhou people pronounce the character [黃] (huáng) no differently from the character 王 (wáng, king); only the character [黃] (huáng) in 蟹黃 (xiè huáng, crab roe) and 蛋黃 (dànhuáng, egg yolk) is pronounced like the character 荒 (huāng, desolate), which is also Northernized.

The Northern and Southern dialects are vastly different, so Northern pronunciation in the Wu dialect is very rare; recently, there is a National Language course in elementary schools, which is truly a language that is neither Southern nor Northern; Southerners find it funny, and Northerners find it even funnier; no wonder there are some witty sayings in society, calling it: [Not afraid of heaven, not afraid of earth, only afraid of Suzhou people speaking Mandarin].

Lying 240

— Yong Zi

| Mr. Liao Zhai is the Saint of Lies |

There is a publicly recognized liar in America. It is said that recently, because he told a great lie that Americans consider unprecedented, the governor appointed him as the [Official Liar] and gave him an annual salary of one U.S. dollar to encourage him. The lie told by this [Official Liar] this time is: [He had seen a cat with a wooden prosthetic leg use the prosthetic leg to kill a mouse.] Although these words sound like a lie, to us Chinese people who are used to hearing lies, it is too bland to be worth mentioning. Unexpectedly, Americans, who are more advanced than China in everything, are so naive in their ability to hear lies.

The history of lying in our China, not to brag, not to lie, is even before the many years and eighty-one tribulations that Tang Sanzang experienced. Zhuge Liang borrowing the east wind is even later. If you have to say when there was already history, then it should probably be the Nuwa clan who refined stones to repair the sky. As for complete books of lies, such as "Records of Night Talks," and "What the Master Would Not Discuss," which one is not a complete compendium of lies with a beginning and an end? "Strange Tales from a Chinese Studio" is an even more popular and eternally immortal masterpiece of lies. It is a pity that Mr. Liao Zhai racked his brains and left such a great work of lies that moves the gods and darkens the sun and moon, only for the Chinese people who live by listening to lies to use as reading material for leisure after tea and wine. If Mr. Liao Zhai were born in America, I think the degree of Doctor of Lying would be no problem, of course, he would get it. If universities were to insert a subject of Lying, they would of course invite Mr. Liao Zhai to be a professor, and the annual salary would be tens of thousands of times more than that of the [Official Liar]. Now, if someone were to sort out all the books of lies in China, ask a few returned students to extract the essence, and compile a [Outline of Chinese Lies] to sell in America, not only can it prove that China has a cultural history of thousands of years, raise the status of China a little, but also make a fortune in foreign money, I think that would be a good deal that kills two birds with one stone.

Eighteen Twin Pregnancies 241

— Man

| Panoramic View |

I remember one day, on a picture advertisement of a certain tobacco company, "Overseas Strange Tales," I saw a strange story, saying that there was a pair of twins, their father, grandfather, and maternal grandmother were also twins. I am now introducing you to a similar strange story for your after-dinner conversation.

Sun Zhilu of the Qing Dynasty, a native of Hangzhou, wrote "Second Shen Yelu," named "Second Shen" because the book was based on the period from the Ming Dynasty Hongwu Wushen to Chongzhen Renshen. One section recorded that:

[Yang Qi, a resident of Ningguo Prefecture, his wife, Yu Shi, married at the age of eight or more and became pregnant. She was very large. After giving birth, she gave birth to twins. Not long after, she became pregnant again and gave birth to twins again. From then on, she became pregnant in succession, from the age of sixteen to fifty-two, with a total of eighteen pregnancies. Each pregnancy was twins, all boys, with a total of thirty-six children, all of whom grew up and none of them died young. This woman also had no illness and lived to a ripe old age and died.

I think this Yu Shi is really a strange person, she would get pregnant eighteen times, and every time she gave birth, it was always two boys. Now, young mistresses can't even manage one child, and they are already complaining endlessly. Let's think about this Yu Shi, in the later pregnancies, when giving birth, the older ones were enough to help, so she wouldn't be too tired, but in the beginning, she had to take care of at least eight children. We really can't guess how she lived her life at that time, ha ha.]

The world now is fundamentally a contradictory world, so on the one hand, some people are calling for birth control, and on the other hand, most countries are drafting regulations to encourage childbirth. It is said that a wealthy man in the United States took out a sum of money as a bonus to reward the small family with the most children. There is a family where the couple already have twenty-five children of all sizes, and they have a good chance of winning the award, etc., but compared with Yang Qi's [thirty-six], it is like a great wizard seeing a small wizard, and is far behind.

Money and Flesh 242

— Min Chonglou

| Deformed Relationship |

In this era, money and flesh have developed a close relationship like magnets and iron.

Having flesh without money leaves the flesh with no room to move. Having money without flesh does not reveal the miracle of money.

Rickshaw pullers do not suffer with their two legs, and they cannot eat fried dough sticks and sesame cakes. Prostitutes do not cater to patrons, and they will be whipped and scolded by their madams. Is this not flesh acting for money? Rich magnates hire a few foreign bodyguards, afraid that kidnappers will not retreat three houses. Originally, crime is punishable by death, but they are acquitted because of heavy bribes. Is this not money revealing its miracle?

[Face] is flesh, so money can make it show ... laughter. [Heart] is flesh, so money can make it produce sorrow, joy ... emotions. The flesh of all adults, gentlemen, fashionable men and women, peddlers ... has a close relationship with money.

Some people say, [In this day and age, the relationship between money and flesh is not worth making a fuss about.] But I think those traitors who fawn on the enemy for money, and the merchants who sell contraband goods for money, endanger the public for their own private interests. This kind of relationship between money and flesh cannot be regarded as a bland story!

In a deformed society, let money and flesh develop towards a deformed relationship!

Marriage Quotes Little Xiang 243

A good wife makes a good husband. — English proverb

Novel Photography 244

— Mo Yi

Da da da da... Da da da da da da da... Da da da... Da da... Da...

Zhang Rongjiu knelt in the middle, finding it difficult to break out, so he had to follow the crowd in a chaotic squeeze. He hadn't taken a few steps when he heard a series of increasingly intense da... da... da... sounds, and flashes of light flickered before his eyes; the people in front were actually retreating backwards, while the people behind were pushing forward forcefully; he was knocked to the ground by the people in this way. As soon as he fell to the ground, he felt heavily pressed down by who knows how many people, unable to breathe, and his mind buzzed, not understanding where he had ended up.

[Hum... Hum... Yo... Yo...]

[Ah... Ah... Hum... Hum...]

[Damn it, it really hurts... It burns...]

[I, your father, will be a man again in twenty years, and it won't matter if I kill a few dwarfs, not counting as humans...]

Zhang Rongjiu lay on the ground, half-conscious, hearing cries and screams from the east and moans from the west: the people pressing on him had probably been hit by bullets, their bodies twitched twice, and blood rained down on his face, and the blood on the ground flowed from all directions to his side, dyeing him a blood-soaked person.

Da... Da da... Da da da... Da da da da da da da... Da da da da da... Da da da da da... Da da da da da da da... Da da da... Da da... Da...

In yesterday's [Photography] fifteenth line, [Mom, you've lived for eighty-some years...] the words [you've lived] were mistakenly typeset as [lived in seclusion], hereby corrected.

New Inventions 245

Two Amazing Inventions in Military Weapons 246

— Shi Shi

The effectiveness of searchlights in military affairs is extremely significant, which is generally known. However, the disadvantage of ordinary searchlights is that they are often exploited by the enemy during war, using the light to find the path, and instead become the target for enemy fire, so military strategists often consider this a regret in the practical use of searchlights. In 1927, the famous British scientist Mr. I. L. Baird, in view of this, spent years of hard work and painstaking research, and invented a non-light searchlight, English name Noctovihior. Its structure and form are no different from ordinary ones, but its light emission is not perceivable by ordinary human vision. Examining the principle of its invention, it purely adopts the red line Infra-recray in sunlight as the largest element. We people deeply know that the sunlight band includes seven colors: red, orange, yellow, green, blue, indigo, and violet, and according to research by optical scientists, outside the violet light, there is also a kind of [ultraviolet rays], and outside the red light, there is a kind of [infrared rays]. Both of these types of light are not visible to ordinary people. Ultraviolet rays have a very strong chemical effect, which can treat diseases and can also identify the authenticity of goods. Recently, it has been discovered that ultraviolet rays have the effect of secret communication. Infrared rays have extremely strong light power, also known as heat rays. Its light wave is about one hundred and sixty times longer than the red light line. Mr. Pete installed a rubber light-gathering device in front of the searchlight, collecting various light rays, and only allowing infrared rays to be emitted. At the same time, he also used the efficiency of the photoelectric tube PhotoElectricCell to make the object being shot appear in our eyes, without the slightest error. The invention of this searchlight has caused military scientists around the world to lose color in comparison. Recent test results show that the [transmittance] of its light is increased by more than three hundred times compared to ordinary searchlights, and it is not hindered by dim nights or heavy fog. When one side uses this light in combat, and at the same time supplements it with observation and aiming equipment, such as the latest invention of the electric linkage observation instrument; [Victor predictor] Vicdercpredictir and other items, it is enough to make bullets hit without fail, eliminating strong enemies invisibly.

Killer sonic waves can be called [dead sound]. This invention is based on Maxwell's killer rays [death rays]. It is like the invention of [television] after the invention of the telephone. According to the reason why our human ear organs can feel external sounds, the sound waves are transmitted to the eardrum and touched the auditory nerve through the vibration of the air. The difference in the frequency of sound wave vibrations distinguishes the clarity, lightness, and weight of the sound. Generally, musicians use the ratio of sound wave vibration frequencies and the arrangement of vibration numbers to develop the theory of tone intervals and scales. Acoustic scientists have studied the relationship between sound wave vibration frequency and hearing, and know that if the sound wave vibration number is less than sixteen times per second, the human ear cannot distinguish it, and the human ear cannot feel it if the vibration number is less than 40,000 times per second. The sensory power of the ear canal is limited, and sounds that are too fine or too loud cannot be heard. Due to the enlightenment of this kind of precedent, most scientists pay more attention to the realm of lower or higher vibration numbers, and think about exploring something. Most recently, two Americans, Hutter and Romis, were appointed as professors of experimental physics at Johns Hopkins University in the United States. They specialized in researching sound waves with the highest vibration frequency, namely [high-frequency sound waves], and empirically tested the potential and effectiveness of this high-frequency sound wave. After several experimental results, it was found that the possibility of killing people if the sound wave vibration number is more than 100,000 times per second. Therefore, Hulao and his colleagues [American United Electric Company] manufactured various experimental machines, and invented a death sound with a sound wave vibration number of more than 700,000 times per second. This kind of sound wave has the intensity of scorching heat and fierce combustion. No matter what kind of tough material, such as crystal, it will immediately become powder. There is also a kind of severe chemical reaction. Knives, such as mercury and water, absolutely cannot be chemically reacted at ordinary times, but through the strange effect of this kind of high-frequency sound wave, the two liquids are mixed to form [mercury mixture]. When human and other animal blood cells encounter this kind of sound wave, they are immediately destroyed and destroyed, and life is instantly cut off. Mr. Chen Gan's Qinghe Magazine, edited by the publishing industry, has been published in the sixth issue. The reviews include an article by Mr. Chen entitled Xigafeinanxia. Other works, such as Mr. Zheng Shuwen's Chronicle, Yao Ji's Legend, Xiang Lu Diary, and six kinds of celebrity notes, are quite valuable, and there are many textual research materials.

Money Industry Market to Resume Afternoon Trading Tomorrow 260

The money industry market trades in premium drafts and loans. There have traditionally been morning and afternoon markets every day. For the past ten or so days, due to the beginning of the abolished lunar new year, all industries have been at a standstill, and the time for operations has not yet arrived. To save on procedures, only the morning market has been open. Once business opportunities develop, afternoon market trading will resume. This is a customary practice of the past. It has been very quiet these past two weeks since January 25th, (that is, the so-called New Year's Day and Lantern Festival). However, in the past few days, due to the abolition of the tael and the conversion to yuan, banks urgently need to implement this and must prepare sufficient amounts of silver dollars to be able to circulate them. But there is no way to buy or sell them. Although the morning market is quite inconvenient, some have proposed to start the afternoon market early. In response to the needs of the times, the Money Industry Market, after deliberation by the Market Committee, approved the resumption of afternoon market trading tomorrow (that is, the 10th, which is also the sixteenth day of the first lunar month) to facilitate the turnover of various industries and to facilitate bank transactions.

Because the money industry was slow to submit folds, most major players did not take action. Various inland groups also have not yet made any moves. Over 8,000 Boxes of Metal Tinplate Arrived Yesterday 273

The metal market situation was still peaceful yesterday. Although transactions from customer groups and factories were not very enthusiastic, purchases from the construction group were still fairly satisfactory. The market conditions for various goods, due to overseas telegrams yesterday reporting rumors of a sharp rise, people's hearts were consolidated and unwilling to easily open prices, so it was a good scene, greatly different from the past. Colleagues searching for spot goods from foreign firms felt increasingly frequent. It was heard that several foreign firms, such as Devi and Tianshang, sold quite a lot of spot goods yesterday, with tinplate being the most numerous.

Yesterday, 8,400 boxes of large and small tinplate arrived at the New Taikoo Warehouse, 3,000 of which were from the oil company, and 2,000 boxes were transferred to Hankou, so only 3,000 boxes could be sold in this port.

Also, according to a telegram from London on the 8th, copper rose slightly by 0625, electrical copper fell by 125, tin fell by 0625 to 375, lead fell by 125, the March term fell by 0625, zinc rose by 0625, antimony did not change, pig iron fell by 2.6, to 65.00.

European Metal Factories Unite for Major Price Increase 274

According to secret news from major foreign firms such as Anlichie Cheng, the major metal factories in various European countries, including Britain, Belgium, Germany, and France, are now formally uniting on a large scale to prepare to raise metal prices by 22% to 30%, and the accurate date of implementation is scheduled to be on the 13th of this month. Therefore, the arrival price of old iron products has already risen by half a gold pound, new goods have increased by one pound, and white iron goods have increased by one and a half to two pounds.

Sugar Market, Chaoqing and Shantou Stocks Empty 275

Yesterday, the sugar market was stable with a continued rise in benchmark prices. The guild's price for 24 raw brown sugar and first white was 15 taels and 7 qian. No one accepted it, and later there were slight transactions at 15 taels and 6 qian and a half. No. 20 medium brown sugar and white was 15 taels and 3 qian, No. 89 Dutch red was 12 taels and 3 qian and a half. On the Hanxing side, Jardine Matheson threw out 200 tons of March No. 24 raw white, with the price at 4 yuan 1 jiao and a half Dutch currency, new rules. Other firms were also willing to continue to throw out, so the market was flat. The Jianbang firm continued to open a batch of Di Qing sugar, with the price at 9 taels and 5 qian. The Jian Bing Shuangshi brand opened at 12 taels and 2 qian per shua. Because Di Qing sugar sales were not smooth, traders watched and did not advance, so there were no transactions. However, according to a letter from Shantou, the previous goods had been exhausted, and subsequent batches were never received, the base was quite firm, and the market situation had a divergent trend. Attached is the New York telegram of the 7th, the spot price was 6 jiao 5 fen 625, unchanged. The futures for March, July, December, and January were up 3 pounds each, and May was up 4 pounds, September was up 2 pounds. Also, according to a London telegram, March was up 2 and a half pence, to 4.275, May was up 2 pence 75, to 5.3, and August was up 2 and a half pence, to 5.575. Java white sugar was still 7.750, (all of the above are calculated at 120 pounds).

Seafood Sea Cucumber Plummets One or Two Dozen Taels 276

| New Mushrooms Still Popular with Customers |

The sea cucumber market in various producing areas is very stable, and the inventory in Shanghai is not thick, but because customer sales are sluggish, the price has gradually declined. Yesterday's listed prices were Jiajiaxi six-branch white bottom boots sea cucumber at 128 taels, eight-branch at 124 taels, twelve-branch at 103 taels, sixteen-branch at 84 taels and 5 qian, four-branch black wrinkled sea cucumber at 210 taels, five-branch at 190 taels, six-branch at 165 taels, two-branch Jinshan Meihua sea cucumber at 162 taels, four-branch at 147 taels, six-branch at 123 taels and 5 qian, two-branch Jinshan Wuyan sea cucumber at 108 taels, four-branch at 95 taels, six-branch Li Huiyan sea cucumber at 56 taels, eight-branch at 52 taels and 5 qian. Compared to the market in the winter of last year, each grade fell by 10 to 20 taels, and the firm's purchase appetite was weak. If customer sales do not improve, there is little hope for a temporary recovery.

New mushrooms from various sources continue to arrive recently. Yesterday, a large area of Tunxi high-quality goods opened at 144 taels, medium-grade at 132 and 3 taels, and low-grade at 118 taels. Fujian goods ranged from 142 taels and 5 qian to 126 taels. Chen Jian mushrooms were 115 taels. Transactions on this street were quite strong, and the goods were sold as soon as they arrived, with few remaining.

Business Sutra (7)

Weight of Cotton Bales 277

The packaging of domestic cotton varies from place to place. Shanghai Huoji, domestic cotton is 125 catties per bale and wrapped in white cloth. The packaging of cotton from Taicang, Changshu, etc. is the same as above. Zhejiang Yuyao cotton is 60 catties per bale, two bales are combined into one pair, totaling 120 catties. Jiujiang cotton and Anqing cotton both use wooden frames, each piece weighing 300 pounds, totaling 215 catties. Shandong cotton also uses wooden frames, each piece weighing only 200 pounds, totaling 150 catties. (Wooden frames are tied with iron wire and hemp rope by villagers and are not as strong as machine-packed bales.) Tianjin cotton is the same. The rest of Shaanxi cotton mostly uses foreign frames, each piece weighing 500 pounds, totaling 375 catties. Tongzhou cotton is wrapped in white cloth, with each bale weighing 125 catties (calculated at 75% per pound).
