Free Talk

Life and Living (II) 301

— Li Huiying

As the wheat sprouts emerged from the soil, A-rong's mother abandoned the young couple and went to sleep beneath the earth. A brand-new earthen grave was piled up in the southwest corner of their yard. The hot tears cried by the son and daughter-in-law almost scalded the weeds next to the grave, but the dead person still could not be revived by crying.

They were extremely sad.

[Don't think about it anymore, you can't bring her back by thinking.]

The wife, seeing A-lao unhappy, comforted him. Similarly, A-rong also comforted her:

[You don't need to worry anymore either, anyway, she couldn't have stayed with us for life.]

Such mutual consolations eased their sorrow.

However, both of them had the same question, which was:

Why did Mom die so quickly, in just three days?

Later, both of them had the same answer:

[Why? Because we didn't have extra money!]

Fortunately, a new miracle occurred a month later. This unexpected event increased their infinite joy, and this joy later overcame all the sorrow.

A small creature had already occupied a considerable position in A-rong's wife's belly.

This was such a joyful thing!

·············

After the New Year, the green wheat had grown to more than an inch high. It was a clear and peaceful day, the sun shining high. A-rong, barefoot, was digging up mud in the shallow creek. He carried the mud to the wheat field and spread it around, considering it fertilizer. Everyone was taking advantage of this good day to dig.

His feet, legs, body, and even his face were covered with mud, but A-rong didn't pay attention to any of that. He kept digging, one scoop at a time, and after digging, he carried it to the wheat field. A large pit was gradually dug out in the creek, and a large pile accumulated in the wheat field. The weather was still quite cold, but his whole body was itching, and later he was covered in large drops of sweat. He was panting heavily.

After a while, he leaned against the bank of the creek and lay down, his eyes looking at the sky.

There were floating clouds, birds, and the sun in the sky, and he saw them all. Then he lowered his head and looked around at the fields, at the people working in the fields, at the passersby, and at his mother's grave. He stayed there for a while.

When he stood up and was about to go down into the creek to dig mud again, he suddenly saw his wife spreading mud in the wheat field, and she had already spread a large area, covering the green seedlings with a layer of black stuff. He looked, thought, and realized something was wrong. He hurriedly walked to where his wife was working and asked:

[How long have you been doing this? Go back quickly.]

His wife didn't answer, but looked at him, at the mud all over his body, and smiled.

[Don't tire yourself out, don't you know?] he said again.

The eyes of both of them involuntarily focused on one place, the place that contained a small life.

[Go back, I'll definitely finish it by tonight,] he said, becoming insistent. (To be continued)

Welcome, Antiquities 302

— Xuan

Ever since the cannons of Japanese imperialism captured [The First Majestic Pass Under Heaven] in four hours, the great officials and gentlemen have been worried about the antiquities in the cultural city of Beiping. Now it's all right. Pingjin has not yet fallen, but the antiquities have already been packed into boxes waiting to be transported; it is said that there are three thousand large wooden boxes in total, requiring four trains to move them; in that case, should Pingjin fall in the not-too-distant future, but the antiquities remain unharmed, the great officials and gentlemen can at least plead innocence before their ancestors.

Although there are as many as three thousand boxes of antiquities, in the end, there are only three thousand boxes, and four trains can carry them all away. This cannot be compared to the land of Pingjin, which cannot be transported away. As for the common people of Pingjin, the hundreds of thousands of common people, it is even less necessary to plan for them; they have their own legs!

Moreover, in terms of value, the common people are hateful, while the antiquities are precious. Haven't you seen the many books written by foreign dignitaries about the ancient Chinese kingdom? They mock the pig-like Chinese common people, but praise the unparalleled Chinese antiquities! If valuable antiquities were lost for the sake of worthless common people, wouldn't that be a lament for the foreign dignitaries, and wouldn't it cause international ridicule? Therefore, we common people cannot but thank the great officials and gentlemen for their painstaking efforts in serving the country!

However, the Japanese imperialists with ulterior motives do not seem to let go just because the antiquities of Beiping have been moved away. They are hurriedly increasing their troops to the border of Rehe. We use trains to transport antiquities, and they use trains to transport troops. The common people of Pingjin see the antiquity trains heading south, but do not see the troop trains heading north, and they hear that the Japanese army is pressing in step by step. Their abandoned and helpless tears can only be swallowed into their stomachs. Unfortunately, the mechanical civilization of the foreign devils has not yet reached omnipotence. Otherwise, using a huge crane to lift all the national treasures of the ancient Chinese kingdom, such as the Three Seas and the Imperial Palace in Beiping, the Confucius Forest in Qufu, and the Sun Mausoleum in Nanjing, all together to the highest peak of the Himalayas, so that the great officials and gentlemen could safely guard there [for long-term resistance], wouldn't that be an unparalleled feat!

However, the fact that there are already four trains of antiquities waiting to be transported is indeed an amazing scheme. After the common people are moved to tears of gratitude, they should shout three times... Long live the antiquities!

The New System of Weights and Measures 303

— Peng Jiahhuang

We Chinese people have our own national essence. For example, the calendar follows the old method, and the waxing and waning of the moon can be used to deduce the new moon and full moon. In that case, there is nothing wrong with the [lunar calendar]. If it must be changed to the [solar calendar], it would be better to change it completely. However, after so many years, it is still unclear which is [lunar] and which is [solar]. Government offices, companies, and banks follow their [solar calendar], while landladies, nannies, and the like follow their [lunar calendar]. Recently, with the exception of foreigners, whether they are new or old figures, they all have some [lunar] air, and [lunar] calendars are also very popular. Almost even many modern female students have memorized the [first day] and [fifteenth day] of the lunar month, and can accurately match them to the corresponding dates in the [solar calendar] without any mistakes. But like in the past few years, when the [lunar calendar] was banned and lunar calendars could not be bought, there was no way to deduce the new moon and full moon. If you ask a woman, [Is today the...?], she can very precisely calculate that in ten or twenty days it will be [Dragon Boat Festival] or [Double Ninth Festival], and she should prepare zongzi and festival gifts. Why do they want to preserve this national essence? In fact, speaking plainly, it's worth a few dollars. Because some months in the [solar calendar] have thirty-one days, while the [lunar calendar] has at most thirty days per month. Collecting rent and receiving wages are still more cost-effective with the [lunar calendar]. If there were no [solar calendar], there would be no way to cheat.

Speaking of weights and measures, there was originally a [system], but the previous [system] was too old and had flaws, so there should be a [new] one. For example, a vegetable vendor says that his is the official [system], sixteen taels. Maybe it is sixteen taels, but we always think that his is fourteen taels, twelve taels. No, only my twenty taels, twenty-four taels, is right. But no one is willing to exchange.

The [new] [system] is of course better than the [old] one. But according to the report from the Municipal Weights and Measures Inspection Office to the Social Bureau: [ ...changing to the new system ...taking the opportunity to raise prices ...and fabricating official instrument titles, deceiving and peddling ...will cause this city's handling of weights and measures administration, which is inherently beneficial to the people, to be tarnished with the name of profit-seeking, affecting its credibility... ] What should we do if this continues?

The [new] [system] has just started, and it is already [old] again. I think it would be best to have an even newer [system], a perpetually flaw-free, updated [system]. Otherwise, we might as well close the [new] foreign schools and encourage people to read more of the [old] sages' books: [Cultivate your heart, refine your character, regulate your family, and then you can govern the country and bring peace to the world.]

Crossroads of the Times and Love (Continued) 304

— Zhang Ziping

[Why isn't there any news yet?]

He became anxious. He looked at his watch again, and only seven more minutes had passed since he looked at it last time. He sighed softly again.

[It's better not to pay attention to such a boring woman! She's not worth me being so upset for! I want to remain chaste for Peizhu!]

He tried his best to suppress his desires again, closing his eyes. He thought that being able to fall asleep like this would be fortunate. Everything would be settled tomorrow.

He drifted in and out of consciousness for a while, then seemed to be startled awake by something unexpected. He looked at his watch again, it was almost half past one.

[This is truly unreasonable! She dares not come up to see me! I'll have to question her properly tomorrow! If I don't get a satisfactory answer, I'll give her an ultimatum. The final measure is to move out of this house!]

The more he thought about it, the angrier he became. He was mentally drafting how to word his questions to her tomorrow.

[She is a very cunning woman. Even if I question her tomorrow, there will be no results. She will definitely say the same thing as last time, that she saw I was asleep and didn't dare to disturb me... This is just infuriating!]

He turned over and sat up, put the long cotton robe hanging on the back of the chair on his back, put on his slippers, and decided to go downstairs to inquire about her movements.

[Wouldn't it be embarrassing if she saw me?... It doesn't matter! I have a legitimate reason to come down, if I see her, I'll just go to the bathroom to relieve myself!]

At the top of the stairs, he looked down to the second floor, but it was all dark.

[Are they all asleep? That's good, let me go down and see what she and that Japanese guy are doing... ]

Using the light from his room, he felt along the edge of the stairs and walked down to the second floor. He stood at the door of Mrs. Tsuruko's room, pressing down on his racing heart, and listened for a moment to the movements inside, but he couldn't hear any sound. He concentrated and listened carefully again, and there seemed to be a slight snoring sound inside, but he couldn't tell if it was from one person or two.

How to Avoid Tragedy After Marriage? 305

— Gu Fengcheng

Love is like drinking wine, the taste is sweet and rich, the color is bright red: in the process of love, one can sometimes forget everything.

The ultimate goal of love is marriage, and marriage is the final destination of love. Young men and women in the midst of passionate love are constantly pursuing the goal of marriage. But the question arises, are love and marriage really two separate stages? Some say: marriage is the graveyard of love; others say: marriage is the home of love. Is the life of love happier, or is the life after marriage happier? This question has been discussed by many people, but no conclusion has been reached so far, because each person's views are different, and each person's life is also different. Some people are happier after marriage than when they were in love, while others are very good when they are in love, but everything is shattered after marriage.

Of course, the luckiest people are those who are happier after marriage than when they were in love; the question that I want to raise here is that I have seen many people who are often very passionate and happy when they are in love, but as soon as they get married, a tragedy occurs.

How to avoid tragedy after marriage is of course a question worth discussing.

Now, based on my personal observations and the experiences I have gained from several friends, the tragedies that occur after they get married are nothing more than the following:

First, in love, everything is centered on love, and both sides only have emotion and no reason. Each person's personality and temperament are shrouded in passion. Even if he has a bad temper, he will never flare up in front of his lover. He will definitely be as gentle as a little lamb and as happy as a little angel. In that height of overflowing passion, each person's bad temper and bad habits are hidden. Therefore, in passionate love, it is difficult to discover the differences in each person's personality when everything starts with emotion. However, it is different after marriage, because married life is relatively calm and stable. Each person's personality and temperament also erupt as the marriage period lengthens. What could be sacrificed in love often cannot be sacrificed after marriage. The temper that could not be seen in love completely erupts after marriage. From then on, a tragedy occurs between the two, often leading to divorce due to differences in personality and character after marriage. This is the most common tragedy that occurs after marriage.

Second, the difference in each person's living habits. This is also often difficult to discover for a while during the love period, and is not noticed by both parties. Because the two sides have not lived together during the love period, then the differences in the living habits of the two sides are often not easily discovered. Moreover, during the love period, even if there are any differences in the living habits of each person, both sides are willing to compromise and sacrifice for each other. For example, the man's life is active, and the woman's life is quiet. During the love period, if the man often asks the woman to go out and play, even if the woman sometimes feels unwilling, but in order to make their love without any regrets, she often sacrifices her own habits and agrees to the man's request. This kind of sacrifice is often unwilling after marriage. For example, if the woman already has a child, she needs a calmer and more stable life. If the man continues to ask her constantly, she will unceremoniously reject him. At that time, the man will feel disappointed and disillusioned, thinking that his lover is not as lively and lovely as before. If this continues, it will also destroy the future of their love. This is the second type of tragedy that may occur after marriage.

(To be continued)

On Smoking 306

— Wu

Since I am a smoker myself, I have many strange understandings about smoking.

After eating, you must smoke, when using the toilet, you must smoke, you can smoke while reading, and you need to smoke even more when writing articles. When talking with friends, you must smoke, but when talking with your lover, you can't smoke; the reason is very simple, because many women will mostly be saddened to tears by the smoke.

Many people think that smoking is just a kind of life philosophy, and it only needs to be embellished in front of people, so there is no need to be serious. However, there are also many people who regard smoking as an essential element of life, and they cannot be without it for a moment. Therefore, when he gets on the tram, he clearly sees the words "No Smoking" written on the tram, but he insists on smoking, and spews it at people's faces. From this, it can be known that this kind of person's addiction to smoking is also very strong.

There are all kinds of cigarettes, perhaps because they are different for different people. For example, gentlemen must have cigars, artists must have tobacco pipes, old men mostly like [Gold and Silver], young men love to smoke [Aiqing], old masters should smoke [Gao Er Fu], young masters should smoke [Meili], (English name is My Dear), rich people should smoke [Chesterfield] brand, and poor people can only eat [Kotou] brand made of cigarette butts. As for the current critical and dangerous autumn when the national crisis is deepening and foreign insults are becoming more and more urgent, we patriotic people should not only sincerely obey orders to promote domestic goods and not smoke [Shenxian] (said to be inferior goods), but also unite and cooperate to smoke [Hero Brand], moreover, [smoking to save the country] may not be a way to save the country.

Writing freely, many words are not carefully chosen. Finally, I respectfully recite [Amitabha!]

Science

The Prime Mover of the Future 309

— Yu Heng

This is a problem that humanity depends on for survival and that must be solved: Where will we get our prime mover in the future? What if electricity and trams stop working, all the chimneys no longer belch black smoke, and engines and motors all fall into slumber, if coal and petroleum are all used up?

This day is finally coming. Some people have already estimated that the coal on Earth is only enough to maintain us for one or two thousand years. If the use of coal expands even more, it might not even last a thousand years! The situation with oil is the same.

This is not only a problem for the future, but it is becoming a problem for the present. Some countries rely entirely on foreign imports for coal and oil. Japan is one such example. Deeds of aggression often arise from this problem.

If the end of the prime mover really comes, where will violent force go to seize coal and oil? Moreover, the sharp weapons of force - warships, tanks, and airplanes - cannot function without the prime mover.

The first new prime mover is water power. In the United States, it can be said that it has been fully utilized. According to the report of the engineers of the Construction Committee, the Yangtze River in our country can generate four million horsepower from Chongqing to Yichang. When the hydropower plant is established in the future, its effectiveness will certainly be great, and the amount of coal saved will be considerable.

Second, is the use of the power of the tides. Anyone who has been to Qiantang to see the tide will think about the greatness of the power of the tides! The United States is now planning how to use tidal power in the Bay of Fundy.

The third is the sun. Have you ever thought about how much heat the sun emits? In every square mile of the tropics, the heat it gives off is equivalent to 10,000 tons of coal! As for how to collect this heat source, there is still no perfect method.

Finally, there is synthetic fuel, most of which is made by combining carbon monoxide and hydrogen under pressure and temperature. Carbon monoxide is a by-product of several major industries, but hydrogen is a gas, and the necessary pressure and temperature all rely on the existence of other prime movers, so it is not considered a complete success. However, the characteristics and effectiveness of this fuel are great, usually twice as strong as gasoline.

We cannot help but ask a question: Will these new prime movers have a day when they run out? In short, the existence of water power and tides is completely related to the power of the sun. If the sun is not destroyed, water power and tides will not rest. If the sun is destroyed, even if we have the prime mover, what can we do?

Women Are Lovely Late Bloomers 311

— Exploring from Women's Names —

Women are lovely, exploring from good names, what Yang Wanyu, Xi Yueqin, Ping Huiyu, Pan Baozhu, Li Suzhen, Jin Xiufen, Wang Renmei, Dai Xiaolong, Huang Jinhua, Jin Lijiao... You see [Jade]! [Qin]! [Pearl]! [Zhen]! [Fen]! [Mei]! [Li]! [Jiao]! How touching and endearing!

American youths - men - have two major idols, namely gold and beauty. If you want to get a lover, first ask if you have gold? If you want gold, first ask if you have learning? With learning, it's not difficult to earn money.

The culture of the world, in fact, is all for the lovely white woman behind the scenes.

Having money, being a what-ever-leader, beautiful young women, it's not a problem, you can find a way to get them, a poor scholar can't even get a pockmarked yellow-faced woman easily!

Of course! Women are lovely! It's not difficult to have money! It's not difficult to ask for a beauty, just give money.

Then, women are lovely! Gold is even more lovely.

Foreign youths love gold and love beauties. Chinese youths also love gold and love beauties. However, foreign youths pursue gold and beauties by relying on their own knowledge and talent, using legitimate means. Chinese youths pursue gold and beauties, wanting to make a fortune, corruption, opportunistic, the attitude is not honorable. This is the difference.

In short, although women are lovely, prepare gold first, otherwise you don't know the ways of the world, but listening to the names of women can also quench thirst with plums.
